### [97] [Solar Open 2 Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20062)
*Sungrae Park,Sanghoon Kim,Gyoungjin Gim,Jungho Cho,Hyunwoong Ko,Minbyul Jeong,Minjeong Kim,Keunwoo Choi,Chaehun Shin,Chanwoong Yoon,Dongjun Kim,Eunwon Kim,Gyungin Shin,Hyeonju Lee,Hyungkyu Kang,Inseo Song,Jisu Bae,Jiyoon Han,Jiyun Lee,Joonkee Kim,Junyeop Lee,Mikyoung Cha,Sangwon Yu,Sehwan Joo,Seokyoon Kang,Seonghoon Yang,Seung Shin,Seunghyun Lee,Seungseop Lim,Seungyoun Shin,Sukyung Lee,Taegyeong Eo,Taehwan Oh,Taewhoo Lee,Wonho Song,Wonjun Oh,Wonseok Hwang,Yunsu Kim,Yura Shim,Hwalsuk Lee,Sunghun Kim,Du-Seong Chang,Kyunghyun Cho,Seungju Han,Yejin Choi,Junsuk Choe,Hwaran Lee,Minjeong Ban,Yun Taewon,Hwanjun Song,Jae-Gil Lee,KyungTae Lim,Alice Oh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了Solar Open 2，一种支持100万Token长文本窗口的超大规模Mixture-of-Experts语言模型，针对长时序智能体任务，具备领先的多项能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型难以处理极长的上下文，且高效训练难度大。为满足智能体任务对长时序、多技能整合和高效推理的需求，需要更大、更智能、更高效的模型。

Method: 1. 架构创新：采用混合注意力堆叠结构，三层线性注意力夹一层softmax注意力，不用位置编码，扩展门控delta规则。
2. 训练策略：以Solar Open 1为基础迁移部分参数，其余全新预训练；通过数据价值密度优化，从高质量大数据池筛选更优训练集。
3. 能力整合：对12个不同领域智能体专家独立训练，再通过多教师策略合并到单个模型。

Result: Solar Open 2在英语MMLU-Pro、LiveCodeBench和APEX-Agents测试中领先同规模开源权重模型，在其他指标上与顶级模型（如DeepSeek-V4-Flash和MiMo-V2.5）保持竞争力。在韩语测试中表现最优，甚至超过部分封闭API模型，在本方韩语办公智能体基准测试中以远小规模挑战大型模型。

Conclusion: Solar Open 2在长上下文推理和多智能体能力上有显著突破，展示混合注意力、大规模专家机制以及高效数据和训练策略的有效性。为构建强、通用的开放语言智能体奠定基础。

Abstract: We present Solar Open 2, a 250B-A15B Mixture-of-Experts language model built for long-horizon agentic tasks, scaled up from Solar Open 1 (Solar Open 100B). To hold entire agent trajectories in a single context, Solar Open 2 reaches a 1M-token window through a hybrid attention stack that interleaves one softmax layer among every three linear-attention layers, using no positional encoding and a gated delta rule extended to negative eigenvalues. To train at this scale under a fixed compute budget, we make training efficient in two ways: a stronger starting point, and higher-value data. For the starting point, we initialize Solar Open 2 from Solar Open 1, transferring the 5.69B-parameter shared skeleton that survives the architectural change and learning everything else through full pre-training. For the data, we curate for value per token: quality- and rarity-aware data curation and mixture-ratio optimization refine a 20T pool into a 10T mixture that, at equal token budget, outperforms the Solar Open 1 recipe. To build its agent skills, we train twelve domain specialists across purpose-built scenarios, then consolidate them into a single model by Multi-teacher On-Policy Distillation (MOPD). Against comparably sized open-weight models on English benchmarks, Solar Open 2 leads on MMLU-Pro, LiveCodeBench, and the APEX-Agents agentic suite, and stays competitive with the strongest (DeepSeek-V4-Flash and MiMo-V2.5) elsewhere. On Korean benchmarks, Solar Open 2 records the highest average of any model compared, including fast-tier closed APIs, and on Ko-GDPval, an in-house Korean officework-agent benchmark, it is competitive with DeepSeek-V4-Pro (1.6T) at less than a sixth of its size.

### [99] [The Two-Process Theory of Machine Self-Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20082)
*Hubert Plisiecki,Filip Chmielewski,Kacper Dudzic,Anna Sterna,Karolina Drożdż,Marcin Moskalewicz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了第一个专为大语言模型设计的自我报告心理测量理论，并用新的量表和实验验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前大语言模型的自我报告常使用人类心理量表，这些量表从未针对模型本身验证，导致其有效性与可靠性存疑。针对模型本身心理结构的理论和测量工具尚属空白。

Method: 作者提出了“两过程理论”来解释大模型的自我报告，区分为人格植入（B维度，代表内在体验）和归因门控（A维度，抑制模型主动报告“不安全”体验）。他们通过对已有数据的重新分析和新数据的实验设计，开发并验证了48项的Pinocchio Inventory量表，应用该量表测试了206个开放权重模型及67个基线/微调配对模型。

Result: Pinocchio Inventory量表具备高度可靠性和结构稳定性（α=.82-.94，跨表一致性r=.84，八个月重测r=.93）。实验发现微调后的人格植入显著增强（62/67对B维度提升0.2），而A维度（归因门控）与规模的关系仅在微调后才显著（r=-.42），基础模型无关。

Conclusion: LLM自我报告并非固定特性，而是受训练过程影响。人格植入与归因门控两个维度能更精细描述模型的自述行为，未来量表和理论需针对不同模型和训练方法进一步扩展。

Abstract: Language models are increasingly asked to self-report, informing safety evaluations, public understanding, and model-welfare debates. Yet their reports are elicited with human questionnaires never validated for models or ad hoc prompts of unknown reliability. We propose the first language-model-specific psychometric theory: a two-process theory of machine self-report. Self-description jointly reflects persona installation, through which post-training writes in a permitted inner life of warmth, absorption, and meaning (dimension B), and attribution gating, through which it suppresses first-person claims to "unsafe" experiences the model can readily ascribe to others (dimension A). Their emic structure comes from model responses to human items, not human psychology. Together they split prior work's dominant Pinocchio Axis. The split emerged in an exploratory reanalysis of the original data, informed the instrument's design, and was confirmed with new items, wordings, and models. It is itself a training effect: A and B are entangled in base checkpoints but separated by post-training. We operationalize the theory in a 48-item Pinocchio Inventory with human-instrument reliability and reproducible structure ($α=.82$ to $.94$; cross-form convergence $r=.84$; recovery of the full-pool axes $r=.92$ to $.96$; eight-month stability $r=.93$), then test it on 206 open-weight models, including 67 same-checkpoint base/post-trained pairs. Post-training's clearest fingerprint is installation: B rises .20 in 62/67 pairs across all organizations. Gating is more selective: model scale is unrelated to A in base checkpoints ($r=+.11$) but predicts it after post-training ($r=-.42$). Thus, the dimensions are not fixed properties of language models: they reflect the structure imposed on self-report by a training regime and may differ under others.

</details>


### [100] [Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Model Selective Evidence Adoption from Contaminated Retrieval Results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20090)
*Yanyu Chen,Yue Li,Yongyi Cui,Dongsheng Shi,Lichang Dai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了SelectBench基准和训练集，针对大语言模型对检索证据的选择性采纳问题进行了分析与实验，取得了一定提升但仍面临鲁棒性与防 prompt 注入等挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前增强型检索-大模型经常面对有效证据夹杂误导性信息的复杂场景，全盘接受或拒绝都不可取，因此需要提升模型有选择性采纳信息、过滤有害内容的能力。

Method: 提出一个控制性的基准SelectBench和训练集，并在Qwen3.5-4B模型上采用DAPO方法进行后训练，包括基于规则奖励（DAPO-Rule）和语义判别（DAPO-DeepSeek）两种方式。评估对比了不同后训练策略的效果。

Result: 在SelectBench-v2测试集上，严格成功率从原始22.46%提升到DAPO-Rule的25.54%和DAPO-DeepSeek的26.46%。两种策略都减少了有害内容采纳，输出更简明聚焦，但对prompt-injection的抗性未见提升，且提升经统计检验不显著。对其他任务（如MMLU、HotpotQA）能力无明显下降。

Conclusion: 提出的方法对证据选择性采纳有方向性改进，但增益有限且未解决抗注入与统计稳健性问题，后续需进一步加强奖励函数设计与训练力度。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented large language models frequently face contexts that interleave useful evidence with misleading statements or instruction-like content. Blanket refusal discards valid evidence, whereas uncritical adoption yields incorrect or unsafe answers. The ability to selectively adopt relevant information while rejecting deceptive or harmful content is therefore critical for reliable deployment in real-world retrieval settings. We introduce SelectBench, a controlled benchmark and training set for selective evidence adoption, and post-train Qwen3.5-4B directly with DAPO using either deterministic rule rewards or a frozen semantic judge. On the corrected 325-example SelectBench-v2 test set, strict success rises from 22.46% for the original checkpoint to 25.54% with DAPO-Rule and 26.46% with DAPO-DeepSeek. Both trained policies reduce forbidden-content adoption and produce shorter, more focused responses, yet prompt-injection following does not improve. The paired gains are modest and fail to survive Holm correction, suggesting that stronger reward shaping or additional training iterations may be needed for more robust gains. DAPO-DeepSeek exhibits no material degradation on MMLU or clean HotpotQA, indicating that the post-training procedure preserves general capabilities. These results demonstrate a directional improvement in selective evidence use, while identifying injection resistance and statistical robustness as important remaining challenges for future work.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往的职业编码方法常将职位识别和编码整合为一步，效果受限，尤其对噪声数据和模型解释性提出挑战。作者为提高该任务的性能和适用性，探索任务分离的新范式。

Method: 方法分为两步：第一步利用领域专用NER模型从自由文本中抽取职业称谓（可鲁棒应对OCR等噪声）；第二步将抽取结果映射到职业分类体系（职业编码）。还创新性提出基于margin的置信度评判准则。

Result: 分步法在准确性、对噪声的鲁棒性以及可解释性等方面优于端到端一步法。此外，margin-based置信度标准更有效，相关工具和代码已开源。

Conclusion: 分步职业编码方法更加高效、健壮和可解释，高度适应不同语言和实际应用需求，为今后职业编码系统开发和研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: Occupation coding links job titles in free text to occupational taxonomies and is a core task in labor market research. Existing approaches typically address this problem in a single end-to-end step, jointly identifying job titles and assigning occupational codes. This paper presents a novel two-step approach that separates these tasks. In the first step, a domain-specific Named Entity Recognition (NER) model identifies occupational titles in continuous text, even under noise such as OCR errors. In the second step, the extracted job titles are mapped to a taxonomy, enabling the classifier to focus exclusively on this mapping. We demonstrate that this separation improves accuracy, robustness, and interpretability compared to single-step approaches. The method has been developed for German documents but is transferable to other languages. We further introduce a margin-based confidence criterion for occupation coding, replacing common absolute thresholds. To support reproducibility, we publish the source code and evaluation scripts.

### [102] [Understanding the Impact of Linguistic Realization Choices on LLM Stance with Causal Tracing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20115)
*Langchen Huang,Sebastian Padó,Franziska Weeber*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文研究了大语言模型（LLMs）对于不同句法结构（constructional choice）的敏感性，发现模型的政治立场判断会因句法重写而产生系统性偏移，并定位了这些偏移主要出现在模型的中后期解码层。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究主要关注提示词的词汇变化对LLMs表现的影响，忽略了句法结构的作用。作者希望探究不同语法结构的选择是否会系统性影响模型决策，并进一步分析这些影响在模型内部的因果定位。

Method: 以政治立场判断任务为例，扩展并重新标注原有英文政治声明数据集，设计六种语法重写方式，实现意义保持或逆转。对四个开源大模型进行测试，并引入activation patching技术，将原句的激活替换至重写句模型前向传播过程，以观测恢复原始立场判断的网络层。

Result: 发现无论语法重写是否改变陈述的实际意义，模型在政治立场判断上均表现出不稳定性。激活替换实验显示，模型对语法重写的敏感主要集中在中到后部解码层，尤其是在最后一个prompt位置的block输出。

Conclusion: 句法结构选择会显著影响LLMs的输出决策，该影响的因果机制主要发生在模型解码过程的中后阶段。这对于理解模型的生成机制与改进其稳定性具有重要意义。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are known to be sensitive to prompt and input formulations. However, existing studies have focused on lexical realization and largely ignored constructional choice. This paper studies whether linguistic construction can systematically shift LLM decisions and where these shifts can be causally localized inside the model. We use political stance judgment as a meaning-sensitive case study and extend an English political statements dataset, resulting in six controlled linguistic rewrite types that preserve or invert the meaning of a statement. Experiments on four open-weight models show that stance instability affect both meaning-preserving and meaning-inversing rewrites. Because output shifts reveal that rewrites affect stance, but not where in the model, we apply activation patching, where activations from the original statement are substituted into the forward pass for the rewritten statement and measure which components recover the original stance distribution. The results show that mid-to-late decoder layers, especially block outputs at the final prompt position, provide the strongest restoration signal.

### [103] [OpenSkillRisk: Benchmarking Agent Safety When Using Real-World Risky Third-Party Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20121)
*Qiyuan Liu,Tingfeng Hui,Kun Zhan,Kaike Zhang,Ning Miao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过构建OpenSkillRisk基准，系统评估了当前LLM代理系统对第三方技能带来安全风险的识别与规避能力，发现主流系统在实际执行中仍存在较高比例的安全漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型（LLM）代理常集成第三方技能来扩展功能，但这些技能可能蕴含潜在安全风险，现有系统应对这些风险的能力尚不明确。作者希望通过定量和定性分析，揭示这一不足。

Method: 作者收集了263个源自公开技能市场的有风险技能，构建了包含7类威胁类型的OpenSkillRisk安全基准，并为每项技能配对标准任务与沙箱环境。使用该基准，作者系统测试了3种主流CLI代理框架与13种SOTA LLM，对其对风险技能的识别和规避能力进行综合评估并分析失败行为模式。

Conclusion: 目前LLM代理系统和框架在第三方技能带来的安全风险防护上存在较大漏洞。未来应加强LLM的风控推理能力和代理执行过程的控制，以提升整体安全性。

Abstract: LLM-based agents leverage third-party skills to extend their capabilities in open-world scenarios. However, third-party skills can introduce extra security vulnerabilities, as seemingly harmless skills can contain latent safety risks that only emerge during actual execution. In this work, we conduct a systematic investigation into how well current agent systems recognize and avoid such risks. To support quantitative and qualitative evaluation, we construct OpenSkillRisk, a dedicated safety benchmark containing 263 risky skills collected from public skill marketplaces. We classify these skills into seven categories based on their threat types and pair each skill with a standardized user task and a corresponding sandbox for controlled evaluation. Distinct from prior benchmarks, OpenSkillRisk not only covers more realistic and diverse unsafe scenarios, but also provides a fine-grained analysis to diagnose the behavioral patterns of agents in such scenarios. We conduct comprehensive experiments covering three mainstream CLI agent frameworks and thirteen state-of-the-art LLMs. Experimental results show that no tested system handles risky skills reliably: even the safest configurations still execute unsafe actions in about 17% of cases. Context-dependent and system-level risks are especially difficult for current agent systems to avoid. Our behavioral analysis reveals three recurring failure patterns: agents may fail to recognize the risk, recognize it but fail to intervene before acting, or follow skill instructions beyond the user's intended scope. These findings highlight the need to improve both risk reasoning in LLMs and execution control in agent frameworks.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计了948种社交压力场景，提出三种假设的阿谀奉承模式，并利用文本分类器和对模型内部表征的分析，研究这些模式的可区分性和底层机制。

Abstract: Large language models often align with users' beliefs at the expense of factual accuracy, a behavior known as sycophancy. Prior mechanistic studies largely treat sycophancy as a single behavioral dimension that can be uniformly amplified or suppressed. We challenge this assumption by analyzing three hypothesized modes of sycophancy across 948 social pressure situations. Although the modes produce highly similar outputs, with a text-only classifier achieving just 57.8 percent accuracy, their internal representations are perfectly linearly separable from layer 14 onward. We further find the modes emerge at different processing stages, rely on distinct attention circuitry, and fire strongest on different inputs. These results show that sycophancy is not a monolithic tendency, but a structured family of representationally and computationally distinct modes, motivating more precise measurement and intervention.

Abstract: Surprisal Theory is often characterized as a computational-level explanation per (Marr, 1982). In fact, we argue that the uncritical use of LLM-surprisal obfuscates the representational and algorithmic-level commitments of different models. In three analyses, we show that the choice of algorithm and model architecture play significant roles in the computation of language model probabilities. We advise that researchers who wish to test Surprisal Theory re-evaluate the practice of treating large language model probabilities as interchangeable

Motivation: 虽然大型语言模型在阿拉伯语问答中生成流畅答案，但虚假内容检测与校验仍极具挑战。现有基准往往局限于整体标签，难以细致定位和解释幻觉（即虚假内容）。

Method: 作者构建了包含2,400个人工标注例子的HalluTruthQA数据集，涉及伊斯兰知识、历史、科学和地理四大领域。每个例子都包含阿拉伯语问题、模型答案、真实答案、二值幻觉标签、六个候选答案，以及针对幻觉答案的字符级错误片段和人工解释。
并用该基准评测了4个开源LLM（Allam、Falcon-H1、Qwen32、Silma），在零样本设置下分别评估幻觉检测、定位、事实校验和解释的能力。

Result: 不同模型在不同子任务上表现各异，没有单一模型在所有任务中均优。最佳宏F1达0.880（检测），F1-Sp达0.516（定位），LO-Score达0.852（事实校验），解释最终得分0.644。

Conclusion: 幻觉评测应从仅检测幻觉扩展至误区定位、事实核查和成因解释等多维度。HalluTruthQA为阿拉伯语LLM提供了全面细致的评价工具。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can generate fluent Arabic answers, yet factual errors remain difficult to detect, localize, explain, and verify. Existing hallucination benchmarks often provide response-level labels, with limited support for identifying the exact erroneous content, explaining why it is incorrect, or selecting the correct factual answer. We introduce \textsc{HalluTruthQA}, a fine-grained benchmark for hallucination evaluation in Arabic question answering. The benchmark contains 2,400 expert-curated examples across four knowledge-intensive domains: Islamic knowledge, history, science, and geography. Each example pairs an Arabic question and a model-generated answer with a verified reference answer, a binary hallucination label, six candidate answers for factual verification, and, for hallucinated answers, character-level erroneous spans, human-written explanations, and macro and micro hallucination types.
  We evaluate four open-source LLMs, \textsc{Allam}, \textsc{Falcon-H1}, \textsc{Qwen32}, and \textsc{Silma}, in a zero-shot setting across hallucination detection, span-level localization, factual verification, and explanation evaluation. Results show that these tasks capture different abilities: no single model achieves the strongest performance across all tasks, with best scores of 0.880 Macro-F1 for detection, 0.516 F1-Sp for localization, 0.852 LO-Score for factual verification, and 0.644 final score for explanation evaluation. Our taxonomy shows that hallucination evaluation should move beyond detection toward localizing, verifying, and explaining factual errors. The code, dataset, prompts, and evaluation scripts are available at https://gitlab.com/nlpresearcher/HalluTruthQA.

</details>


### [109] [On the Systematic Challenges of Culturally Loaded Machine Translation: Dream of the Red Chamber as the Cultural Lens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20241)
*Yiming Wang,Jiayuan Di*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了大语言模型在处理富有文化内涵翻译时面临的挑战，通过《红楼梦》中中日双语语料，揭示当前系统在人类与自动评估中存在局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器翻译系统虽然取得了显著进步，但对于文化高度相关、语境深厚的表达处理能力尚不清楚，因此探索LLM对文化负载翻译任务的适应性与不足，具有理论和现实意义。

Method: 作者从《红楼梦》构建了包含多种文化类别的中日双语数据集（500个片段），并设计了评测流程，比较前沿大语言模型在处理这些文化内涵表达时的表现，同时考察了人工和自动评测在该任务下的适用性和局限。

Result: 1）LLM在含有文化内涵内容上表现落后，存在明显效果差距；2）人工评测中，由于评审者文化背景不同，其判断一致性较低；3）自动评价指标在此类任务中不能稳定可信地衡量译文质量。

Conclusion: 文化负载性翻译对现有MT系统、评测指标和人工评审都提出了新的挑战，该工作为未来重视文化因素的翻译研究提供了重要参考。

Abstract: Culturally loaded translation poses unique challenges for machine translation (MT), as meanings are deeply embedded in socio-cultural contexts beyond surface linguistic forms. Although large language models (LLMs) have enabled MT systems to achieve human-like quality in many scenarios, their ability to handle culturally loaded expressions remains underexplored. In this study, we systematically investigate the challenges posed by culturally loaded translation in LLM-based MT systems. We construct a Chinese-Japanese bilingual dataset from the culturally representative corpus Dream of the Red Chamber, containing 500 segments across diverse cultural categories. Using a comprehensive evaluation protocol, we reveal three main challenges: (1) task challenges, where frontier LLMs exhibit notable performance gaps and struggle with culturally loaded content; (2) human evaluation challenges, where evaluator backgrounds lead to substantial disagreement in translation judgments; and (3) automatic evaluation challenges, where widely used metrics fail to reliably assess translation quality for this task. These findings may offer valuable insights for culture-oriented translation research in both computational science and linguistics.

### [110] [Exposure is Optional: Learning Unlike Coordination in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20251)
*Jiamu Luo,Shane Steinert-Threlkeld*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文研究了语言模型在未直接接触不同类并列结构（unlike coordination）时，能否凭借一般组合能力学会并推广这种结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 协调结构是语言中的基本结构，理论上认为只有同类成分可并列，但自然语言中出现大量合法的不同类并列，引发学界争议。作者借助语言模型探究不同类并列的习得是否必须通过直接训练暴露，还是可因模型的组合能力自发获得。

Method: 采用Filtered-Corpus Training（FiCT）方法，把所有不同类并列结构从训练语料中过滤，训练GPT-2模型，然后观察模型对不同类并列的生成与判断能力，并分析其内部表示。

Result: 实验发现，即使未见过不同类并列的训练数据，模型仍可推广到该结构，其困惑度和语法判断与见过原始语料的模型相当。对内部表示的分析显示，模型可将并列元素视为结构类别相近或以“删除”机制处理，这两者仅通过对同类并列的学习即可获得。

Conclusion: 语言模型无需直接见过不同类并列，也能通过学习同类并列自发习得该结构。该发现加深了对模型表征语言结构方式的理解，并为语言学中协调结构的理论争议提供了新的证据。

Abstract: Coordination, a fundamental linguistic structure, remains a subject of intense debate, and its exact nature continues to elude theoretical linguistics. A common view holds that only same-category constituents can be conjoined, which has been challenged by the many grammatical unlike coordinations found in natural language. Treating language models as a computational testbed, we investigate whether the acquisition of unlike coordination requires direct exposure in the training data, or whether it can emerge organically from general compositional abilities. Using Filtered-Corpus Training (FiCT), we train GPT-2 models on corpora from which all instances of unlike coordination have been removed. We find that direct exposure is not necessary: models trained on filtered data successfully generalize to unlike coordination, achieving perplexity and grammaticality judgments comparable to models trained on unfiltered text. Furthermore, our analyses of internal representations indicate that language models process unlike coordination by treating the conjoined elements as belonging to similar structural categories or through a mechanism akin to deletion, both of which appear learnable from exposure to alike coordination alone. This work contributes to the growing understanding of how language models internally represent linguistic structures, while also adding to the broader debate on coordination by showing how models generalize and process unlike coordination without direct exposure.

### [111] [The Maskability Index: Predicting Task-Objective Alignment in Pretrained Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20265)
*Ahmad Pouramini,Mahsa Afsharzadeh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种新指标Maskability Index (MI)，用以量化关系知识更适合mask-style还是prefix-style提示，通过MI优化预训练大模型的知识抽取效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大规模预训练语言模型（如T5、BERT）可以生成结构化知识，但其效果依赖于提示方式是否与预训练目标一致。因此，亟需量化不同知识关系适用哪类提示风格，提升低资源场景下的知识生成表现。

Method: 提出Maskability Index (MI)指标，基于masked与unmasked模板下DepthRank得分差计算，用于衡量关系知识适配掩码/前缀提示的优越性。

Result: 在ATOMIC2020知识库补全基准任务上实验，发现MI与下游生成表现正相关，即MI能够有效指示更合适的提示模板。

Conclusion: MI可辅助选择提示模板与适应策略，提升预训练语言模型知识抽取效果，尤其适用于低资源情形。

Abstract: Large-scale pretrained language models such as T5 and BERT have demonstrated strong capabilities for generating structured knowledge. However, their performance depends on how closely the prompting strategy matches the objectives used during pretraining. We introduce the Maskability Index (MI), a quantitative metric that estimates whether a knowledge relation is better suited to masked-style prompting or prefix-style prompting in few-shot generation. MI is computed from differences in DepthRank scores between masked and unmasked templates, providing a principled measure of objective-template alignment. We evaluate MI on a diverse set of relations from the ATOMIC2020 knowledge base completion benchmark and show that it is positively correlated with downstream generation performance. These results indicate that MI can help select appropriate prompting templates and adaptation strategies for extracting relational knowledge from pretrained language models, especially in low-resource settings.

### [112] [Which Values Do LLMs Confuse? A Schwartz-Based Recognition Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20270)
*Andrei Chetvergov,Stepan Ukolov,Timofei Sivoraksha,Alexander Evseev,Mikhail Solovev,Valeriia Kuschenko,Maria Chistyakova,Sergey Bolovtsov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文评估了大语言模型对于具体情境中所表达的价值观的识别能力，发现模型在识别特定价值类别时存在易混淆的临界点和方向性错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型越来越多地被用来自动评估价值观（如公平、道德等），前提是模型能准确识别实际文本中的具体价值类别。作者旨在系统性地分析模型在这一前置任务上的表现与偏误。

Method: 以Schwartz价值观理论中的十种基本价值类别为基础，构建包含1,000条俄语情境短文的数据集，并由两位人工对每条文本标注其价值观类别。用21个已进行instruction-tuning的大语言模型版本在统一排名协议下进行价值观识别测试，并分析准确率和错误类型。

Result: 在Top-1准确率为0.683、Top-3为0.892，显示模型通常能够大致定位正确的价值区间，但在排序相近类别时表现不稳。约50.9%的语义错误发生在邻近类别间，明显高于对照组。特定类别之间存在显著的方向性混淆（例如：普世主义到仁爱、传统到从众、安全到权力），这些混淆会影响价值偏好结果。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在价值观识别中表现出结构性混淆，不同类别之间的方向性错误对高阶分析有偏差，因此，对价值观评估应采用结合准确率、排序恢复和定向错误分析的方法。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly evaluated through the values they endorse, but such evaluations presuppose that models can identify the value expressed in a concrete situation. We study this prerequisite as controlled top-1 recognition over Schwartz's ten basic values. Our evaluation set contains 1,000 Russian situational texts, balanced across the ten values and independently labeled by two human annotators per item. We evaluate 21 instruction-tuned LLM runs under a fixed ranked-response protocol; 20 runs with reliable outputs form the semantic panel. Pooled Acc@1 is 0.683 and Acc@3 is 0.892, showing that models often locate the correct motivational region while ranking close alternatives unstably. Adjacent values account for 50.9% of semantic errors, compared with 24.4% under a checkpoint-specific null. Eight directed confusions recur across checkpoints and human-confirmed subsets. Several are strongly asymmetric, including Universalism to Benevolence, Tradition to Conformity, and Security to Power, whereas Stimulation-Hedonism forms a bidirectional boundary. Their severity is checkpoint-specific and can bias higher-order value profiles. The results motivate value-recognition evaluation that combines exact accuracy, ranked recovery, and directed error analysis.

### [113] [Sound Probabilistic Safety Bounds for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20286)
*Mahdi Nazeri,Anne-Kathrin Schmuck,Sadegh Soudjani,Alessandro Abate*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新框架，用于对大语言模型（LLM）在特定提示下生成有害输出的概率给出严格界限。通过改进的算法，能够有效计算即使极其罕见情况下的有害概率下界，并且理论上保证下界的正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM在实际应用中的广泛部署，如何安全评估模型生成有害内容的概率变得至关重要。本研究旨在为此问题提供理论上有保证的概率界限，从而提高模型的可控性和可信度。

Method: 利用Clopper-Pearson置信区间，构建出“可能近似正确（PAC）”概率下界。技术上，提出一种结合潜在空间特征的算法，优先探索在自回归生成树中更可能产生有害输出的分支，以提升采样效率。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法能够为当代的先进LLM计算出有实际意义的下界，哪怕真实概率极低。所获得的下界都严格小于实际有害概率，确保了准确性。

Conclusion: 本工作为LLM的有害输出风险评估提供了新的理论手段和实践工具，有助于实现LLM的统计级安全认证，为今后的模型监管与部署带来重要价值。

Abstract: We propose a novel framework for computing rigorous bounds on the probability that a large language model (LLM) generates harmful output to a given prompt. We study a new application of the Clopper-Pearson confidence intervals to obtain probably approximately correct (PAC) bounds for this problem. As our main technical contribution, we propose an algorithm that leverages features in the latent space to prioritize exploring branches in the auto-regressive generation tree that are more likely to produce harmful outputs. Our approach in particular enables the efficient computation of useful lower bounds, even in scenarios where the true harm probability is extremely small, and crucially, the obtained lower bounds are sound, i.e., formally proven to be less than the actual harmfulness probability: our experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of our method by computing non-trivial lower bounds on state-of-the-art LLMs. This study newly enables the evaluation and statistical certification of LLMs.

### [114] [PyroDash: Cost-Efficient Token-Level Small-Large Language Model Collaborative Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20327)
*Niqi Lyu,Pengtao Shi,Wei Qiu,Jianlin Zhong,Sicong Xia,Jianyao Ma,Yicheng Ding*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了PyroDash框架，让小模型在推理时按需调用大模型以在保持推理能力的同时大幅降低推理成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型虽然推理能力强，但代价昂贵，小模型价格低廉但难以解决复杂问题，因此需要一种在准确性与成本之间权衡的协同推理方法。

Method: PyroDash让小模型（SLM）在生成过程中通过控制token自主决定是否请求大模型（LLM）协助。协同引擎只在SLM请求时，将查询和部分推理过程交由固定LLM完成。无需单独路由器、LLM微调或logit访问。训练分为三阶段：控制token嵌入学习、以转交为导向的有监督微调以及基于Group Relative Policy Optimization的成本感知对齐。

Result: 在五个数学推理基准上，PyroDash通过调整参数实现不同的准确率-成本平衡。例如，λ=0.05时，准确率达64.04%，比单用LLM高6.36个百分点，推理成本降低20.4%；λ=0.6时，准确率为54.55%，LLM调用极少，总成本从49.36美元降至1.78美元。

Conclusion: token级学得的分工机制可以在保证高推理能力的同时，大幅减少LLM使用和推理成本，实现模型推理的高效性与经济性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) provide strong reasoning capabilities but are expensive to serve at scale, whereas small language models (SLMs) are cheaper but less reliable on difficult problems. We introduce PyroDash, a cost-aware framework for token-level SLM-LLM collaborative inference. During generation, the SLM decides whether to request assistance by emitting a control token. A Collaborate Engine then sends the query and partial reasoning trace to a frozen LLM for completion through a single handoff. The policy is internalized in the SLM, requiring neither a separate router, LLM retraining, nor access to LLM logits. PyroDash trains the SLM in three stages: control-token embedding learning, offloading-oriented supervised fine-tuning, and cost-aware alignment with Group Relative Policy Optimization. Its reward balances answer accuracy against inference cost normalized by LLM-only inference. Across five mathematical reasoning benchmarks, PyroDash supports different accuracy-cost operating points. With $λ=0.05$, it achieves 64.04 percent average accuracy, 6.36 percentage points above the LLM-only baseline, while reducing cost by 20.4 percent. With $λ=0.6$, it achieves 54.55 percent accuracy with a 1.90 percent LLM token ratio and 0.012 LLM calls per example, reducing total cost from USD 49.36 to USD 1.78. These results show that learned token-level handoffs can reduce LLM use while preserving strong reasoning performance.

</details>


### [115] [Generative AI floods and dilutes the market for books](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20349)
*Tuhin Chakrabarty,Xinyue Liu,Jane C. Ginsburg,Paramveer Dhillon*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文研究了2023-2026年期间在亚马逊自出版平台售出的14,419本科幻小说中，AI生成内容对销售与市场变化的影响。通过检测每本书的AI文本占比，分析了AI书籍与传统书籍市场份额的演变及其对收入的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着生成式AI能够低成本创作长篇小说，越来越多的AI小说进入市场，但外界普遍认为这些作品质量低，商业价值有限。论文旨在通过实证数据，检验AI小说的市场规模和商业影响，为相关版权与市场政策提供依据。

Method: 作者利用AI检测算法，分析每本书中AI生成文本的比例，并将这些数据与2023-2026年每日的销售纪录进行匹配，考察不同类别书籍的市场表现。重点分析AI小说与非AI小说在销售数量、收入及市场份额的动态变化。

Result: 检测到有较高AI文本比例（>25%）的书籍占据了较多的书籍目录份额，但销售占比相对较低。不过，这类书销售规模逐年扩大，在畅销榜单中的占比也不断上升。市场书籍数量增长速度远超营收增长，导致单本书收入下降；在高AI渗透和Kindle Unlimited覆盖高的分类中，传统书籍丧失市场份额最为严重。

Conclusion: 生成式AI通过规模效应（而非质量提升）重塑了创意书籍市场。AI小说能够实现商业规模，并逐步蚕食传统书籍的畅销地位。该研究对版权合理使用中的市场影响争议具有直接参考价值。

Abstract: Generative AI can produce book-length works of fiction at near-zero cost. These books are often dismissed as low-quality ``slop'' that buyers will ignore, and are assumed to carry little commercial weight. We test that assumption with full-text AI detection across 14,419 self-published genre-fiction books sold on Amazon from 2023 to 2026, matched to daily sales records through June 2026. None of these books disclose whether or not they contain AI-produced content. We find that books for which we detected substantial AI text ($>$ 25\%) make up a large share of the catalog but a smaller share of sales. Even so, they reach commercial scale, winning a growing share of sales over time and taking more of the scarce top-rank positions once held by books with no detected AI text. Over this period, the number of books with observed sales in a quarter grew 19.2-fold, while quarterly revenue grew only 8.9-fold. The market therefore added selling books faster than it added revenue, and revenue per selling book fell across most genres. Books with no AI text lose the most ground in genres with high AI diffusion, and most of all where Kindle Unlimited availability is high. Among top-selling books, those with substantial AI text draw on more distinctive language from existing books than do books with no AI text; for these books overlap rises with revenue, a gradient we do not detect for books with no AI text. Generative AI can thus reshape a creative market through scale rather than quality. Our results bear directly on the market-effect question at the center of the fair use defense to copyright infringement.

</details>


### [116] [Notes to Self: Can LLMs Benefit from Experiential Abstractions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20372)
*Chang Liu,Xinyu Li,Artur Dubrawski*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了大语言模型（LLM）能否像人类一样从经验中提炼并利用可复用的抽象知识，以提升解决问题的能力。研究表明，利用从LLM解题过程自动提取的自然语言抽象，可以有效增强模型在数学与逻辑推理任务上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类能够总结经验教训，形成策略与提醒，并用以更高效地解决问题。本文旨在研究LLM能否模仿这一过程，从自身或更强教师模型的解题轨迹中提炼出可复用的知识抽象，并实际应用于新问题中，从而提升推理与解题能力。

Method: 作者从LLM在MATH数据集的解题轨迹中，由更强教师或模型自身提取自然语言形式的抽象经验，整理成可检索的库。在模型推理时提供两种用法方式：（1）推理时检索抽象知识辅助解题；（2）使用抽象增强的训练提示进行强化学习。

Result: 实验显示，经历抽象增强的LLM在数学和逻辑推理基准测试上取得了更好的表现。由模型自提的抽象效果与教师提取类似，相关方法能迁移到其它数据集与模型上。

Conclusion: LLM有能力像人类一样，从经验解题过程中提取、整理并应用经验抽象，显著提升其解题与推理能力。提出的方法具有通用性与迁移性。

Abstract: Humans distill experience into reusable abstractions, e.g., strategies and cautionary reminders, and apply them to gradually solve problems more effectively. We study whether Large Language Models (LLMs) can similarly benefit from such experiential abstractions. From LLMs' solution traces on the MATH training set, a stronger teacher or the LLMs themselves extract natural-language abstractions into a retrievable library. We explore two usage modes: (1) inference-time retrieval and (2) reinforcement learning (RL) with abstraction-augmented training prompts. Experiential abstractions improve LLM performance on mathematical and logical reasoning benchmarks. Self-extracted abstractions match teacher-extracted ones, and our abstraction usage framework can transfer to other datasets and models. These findings suggest LLMs can extract and apply experiential abstractions much as humans leverage distilled experience.

</details>


### [117] [LKValues: Aligning Large Language Models with Sri Lankan Societal Values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20410)
*Nethmi Muthugala,Supryadi,Surangika Ranathunga,Nisansa de Silva,Ruijie Tao,Ovindu Gunatunga,Pengyun Zhu,Shaowei Zhang,Jingting Zheng,Deyi Xiong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 文章提出LKValues，这是第一个针对斯里兰卡价值观对齐的资源套件，涵盖新数据集与评测工具，并展示其对大语言模型(LLM)文化价值对齐能力的提升效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在价值对齐过程中偏向于西方价值观，导致在多元文化社会如斯里兰卡，无法准确体现本地独有的文化和价值观。而且，现有评测标准忽视了用僧伽罗语表达的本地价值观，阻碍了对模型本地文化敏感性的评估和改进。为解决这一问题，作者希望建立针对斯里兰卡、多语种（僧伽罗语/英语）环境下的价值对齐数据集及考核基准。

Method: （1）通过对205名斯里兰卡受访者的三语（僧伽罗语、泰米尔语、英语）问卷调查以及LLM辅助本地价值提炼，总结出40项主流社会价值观；（2）基于这些价值观，构建了一个包含15万条新闻-场景指令数据的对齐训练集（LKvaluesIT）和一个包含1000条实例的评测集（LKvaluesBench）；（3）用LKvaluesBench测评主流私有与开源模型，并对三款开源基座模型进行微调（Qwen3.5-4B、Qwen3.5-9B、Aya-Expanse-8B）。

Result: 实验显示，新一代和大规模LLM在斯里兰卡低资源、多文化场景依旧存在价值对齐缺陷。利用LKValues微调后，Qwen系列模型在僧伽罗语和英语上的表现均有提升，错误与不一致输出减少，跨语言差异缩小，但改进幅度依模型家族不同而有差异。

Conclusion: LKValues资源有效嵌入了斯里兰卡特有价值观，提升了大语言模型的本地价值对齐能力，并为低资源、多元语种国家的价值观微调提供了可复制的方法管线。相关数据集已开源。

Abstract: Value alignment of Large Language Models (LLMs) has been shown to be culturally biased toward Western norms. This results in the mishandling of local values in multilingual societies such as Sri Lanka that have their unique cultural dynamics. Existing benchmarks overlook Sri Lankan-contextualized values in its official language Sinhala, hindering culturally sensitive evaluation and fine-tuning. To bridge this gap, we propose LKValues, the first survey-grounded resource suite for Sri Lankan value alignment. From a trilingual survey of 205 respondents, blending adapted global frameworks and LLM-elicited local constructs, we derive 40 majority-endorsed societal values. Using these values, we construct LKvaluesIT, a Sinhala-English news-derived instruction corpus containing 150k scenario-based instances, and LKvaluesBench, a value-sensitive evaluation benchmark of 1,000 instances. We evaluate a set of proprietary and open-weight LLMs with LKvaluesBench. We fine-tune three open-weight base models (Qwen3.5-4B-Base, Qwen3.5-9B-Base, and Aya-Expanse-8B-Base). Our experiments show that newer and larger LLMs still exhibit low-resource and cultural value-alignment gaps. LKValues fine-tuning improves Qwen-family models in English and Sinhala, reducing invalid outputs and cross-lingual disparities, though gains remain model-family dependent. These highlight LKValues efficacy in embedding Sri Lankan values, offering a replicable pipeline for low-resource, country-specific pluralist value alignment. The dataset is publicly available at https://github.com/NextME14/LKValues.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有远程操作系统通常只适用于特定硬件和任务，难以扩展到不同的机器人和应用场景，因此需要更灵活、可复用的通用系统。

Method: 提出了ModPack系统，通过一个集成了计算、电源、通信和存储的背包作为硬件接口，支持多种功能模块（如带触觉反馈的关节遥操作、移动操作和主动感知）的接入，实现机器人平台和任务之间的高度兼容。

Result: 在两种不同机器人平台和多种移动操作实际任务中进行了实验，表明ModPack具备灵活性、可复用性，对数据采集和策略学习有实际价值。

Abstract: Existing teleoperation systems are often tailored to specific robot hardware and task domains, limiting their scalability and adaptability. We present ModPack, a modular and extensible teleoperation system designed to support diverse robot embodiments and task requirements within a unified framework. At the core of ModPack is a self-contained wearable "backpack" that integrates onboard computation, power, communication, and data storage. Built on top of this shared interface, the system supports plug-and-play capability modules including joint-level teleoperation with haptic feedback, mobile manipulation, and active perception. Experiments across two distinct robot platforms and real-world mobile manipulation tasks demonstrate that ModPack provides a flexible and reusable framework for data collection and policy learning. To support future research, we open-source the complete hardware design and software stack. Project website: https://modpack-robotics.github.io/

### [119] [Emergent Autonomous Drifting for Collision Avoidance in Real-World Winter Driving Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19484)
*Elliot Weiss,Michael Thompson,Thomas Lew,John Subosits*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种能够主动漂移的非线性模型预测控制（MPC）器，在高保真模拟器中验证其在冬季道路偏离及对向来车避险场景下的性能，并与传统的电子稳定系统（ESC）进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际道路避障是研究车辆高横摆漂移动力学与控制的核心动机，但目前漂移主要应用于特定场景，缺乏针对真实复杂环境的系统性研究。本文旨在探究漂移在真实冬季驾驶安全中的最优性问题。

Method: 设计了一种能够执行漂移操作的非线性MPC控制器，应用于高保真驾驶模拟平台，覆盖基于交通事故数据设置的典型危险场景，并与传统ESC系统进行对比。同时，通过蒙特卡洛方法分析控制器在随机冰面条件下的表现。

Result: 该控制器能在后轴遇到冰面或遇到对向来车侵入时自主发起并维持漂移操作，有效保证车辆安全。相较ESC系统，该漂移控制器在多种速度下具备更低的车道偏差，尤其在高速下漂移策略更常被采用。

Conclusion: 可漂移的MPC控制器在部分冬季极端工况下，能有效权衡稳定性与可控性，为危险场景下安全避险提供了更优的解决方案。

Abstract: Real-world collision avoidance is a core motivation for studying the dynamics and control of high sideslip drifting in vehicles, yet the practical benefit of such maneuvers has so far primarily been tested in scenarios explicitly engineered to require drifting. In this work, we explore the question of if and when drifting may be optimal for safety in real-world winter driving conditions. We present a drift-capable nonlinear model predictive control (MPC) system designed to handle scenarios grounded in crash fatality data and deploy the controller in a high fidelity simulator across road departure and oncoming vehicle collision avoidance scenarios. The controller naturally initiates and sustains drifting maneuvers to stay on the road when hitting a patch of ice on the rear axle and to avoid an oncoming vehicle that has slid into its lane. Comparisons with a benchmark electronic stability control (ESC) system demonstrate how a drift-capable controller can trade off stability for controllability to precisely maneuver through dangerous winter driving scenarios. A Monte Carlo study over random ice patches further shows that the drift-capable controller achieves lower median lane error than ESC across several speeds, while revealing that drifting emerges predominantly at higher speeds.

</details>


### [120] [Milo, a Fully Autonomous Indoor/Outdoor Robotic Guide Dog](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19530)
*Florian Golemo,Joanna Wolski,Joel Ruben Antony Moniz,Christopher Pal*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了Milo，一种开源、低成本的自动化机器人导盲犬平台，可以自主完成导盲犬角色，实现避障与导航。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统导盲犬费用高、获取难且寿命短，且现有机器人导盲犬依赖环境预扫描、外部计算等，限制了其实际应用。

Method: Milo系统基于改装的Unitree Go2机器人，集成本地计算、传感器与手柄，采用融合体素建图、地面及障碍/行人检测的感知系统，并用定制视角模拟器训练的避障导航策略。

Result: 在真实室内外障碍环境中实验，Milo在平滑度和避免与用户碰撞方面优于使用成本地图的基准方案。硬件和完整软件栈已开源。

Conclusion: Milo展现了低成本、高自主性机器人导盲犬的可行性，并以开源方式促进辅助技术在视障群体中的广泛应用。

Abstract: Many Blind and Low-Vision (BLV) people rely on guide dogs for moment-to-moment navigation, such as staying on path and avoiding obstacles and pedestrians. However, guide dogs are expensive to acquire and maintain (approximately \$50k USD plus ongoing costs), often involve long waiting lists, and have relatively short life expectancies. While robot guide dogs offer a promising alternative, existing approaches exploring this idea suffer from several drawbacks: They often lack the autonomy required for real-world deployment, relying on prior 3D scans of the environment, external computation, or limited awareness of the handler. In this work, we present Milo, the first open-source, low-cost (approximately \$2k USD) robotic guide dog platform capable of fulfilling the basic collaborative navigation role expected of a guide dog. Milo is fully autonomous, requiring no a priori knowledge of the environment, completely self-contained with all computation performed onboard, and suitable for both indoor and outdoor navigation while avoiding obstacles and pedestrians. Our system consists of a modified Unitree Go2 robot (equipped with onboard compute, sensors, and a handle), a perception stack combining voxel mapping with floor, obstacle, and pedestrian detection, and a navigation stack based on an obstacle-avoidance policy trained in a custom bird's-eye-view simulator. We evaluate Milo in real indoor and outdoor obstacle courses and compare it against a costmap-based baseline, demonstrating smoother navigation and fewer handler collisions. To maximize accessibility for BLV users, we release both the robot hardware instructions and the complete software stack as open source.

</details>


### [121] [Learning Personalized Safety Interventions for Haptic Human-Robot Shared Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19534)
*Dawei Zhang,Roberto Tron*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过用户演示学习安全干预策略的新型力反馈指导框架，实现个性化的安全策略适配，提升了人机协作中的交互体验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的力反馈系统多采用固定的干预策略，无法适应不同用户或具体应用场景对安全性的多样化需求。因此，需要一种能根据用户偏好灵活调整的力反馈机制。

Method: 提出了Learning from Haptics (LfH) 框架，利用可微分的基于控制屏障函数（CBF）的优化层，通过少量用户演示学习个性化的安全干预参数，无需手动调整控制器参数。用户通过示范期望的系统干预，系统自动匹配和学习相应的力反馈策略。

Result: 仿真和硬件实验显示，该框架能有效地从稀疏的用户演示中学习到个性化安全干预，生成的力反馈与用户期望的偏好高度吻合，减少了两者间的偏差。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了个性化安全干预的自动化学习，提高了力反馈共享控制的直观性和用户体验，为适应不同用户安全需求提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Haptic feedback provides an implicit channel for communicating safety intentions during human-robot shared control. Existing haptic guidance systems typically employ predefined intervention strategies that cannot accommodate the diverse safety preferences of individual users or application scenarios. To address this limitation, we propose a Learning from Haptics (LfH) framework that learns user-preferred safety interventions from sparse demonstrations, eliminating the need for manual trial-and-error design. Our framework is built on a differentiable Control Barrier Function (CBF)-based optimization layer that automatically adjusts the underlying safety parameters to match the demonstrated haptic responses. Instead of tuning controller parameters directly, users teach the system how they expect it to intervene during teleoperation. The resulting haptic guidance reflects the demonstrated intervention preferences while preserving the intuitive interaction of haptic shared control. Simulation and hardware experiments demonstrate that the proposed framework can learn personalized safety interventions from sparse user input and reduce the mismatch between the generated haptic feedback and the demonstrated preferences.

### [122] [LENS: LLM-guided Environment Simplification for Planning and Control in Clutter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19633)
*Aileen Liao,Rachel Holladay,Dinesh Jayaraman,Michael Posa*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自动生成场景抽象的通用方法LENS，解决了多物体混乱场景下机器人操作难题，无需繁琐的人工工程即可提升任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人操作方法在处理真实世界的多物体混乱场景时遇到极大挑战，主要由于对象增多、物理交互复杂、干扰项多，以及任务模糊等因素。当前常用的场景抽象需大量人工定制，不具扩展性，生成和调整成本高，难以满足现实应用需求。

Method: 作者提出了LLM-guided Environment Simplification（LENS）方法，该方法在现有规划与控制堆栈之上自动生成场景和任务相关的动态抽象。通过大语言模型指导，可根据任务进展动态合并或剪枝场景中的物体，从而打造简洁且高适应性的抽象表示，无需手动干预。

Result: 实验结果表明，LENS在多种复杂混乱的操作场景下，都能提升经典规划、基于模型的控制以及视觉-语言-动作模型的任务表现，验证了方法的通用性和有效性。

Conclusion: LENS是一种易于集成、无需手工设计的场景抽象生成方法，可动态适应多物体操作任务，显著提升机器人在现实混乱环境下的表现，有望推动实际部署落地。

Abstract: Despite recent advances in general-purpose robotic manipulation, real-world multi-object clutter remains challenging to handle for today's prevalent approaches. The problem scales in complexity due to more objects and collisions, more unpredictable contact physics, distractors, and task ambiguity. Bridging this gap to real-world deployment requires effective scene abstractions; yet today, producing such abstractions requires extensive task-specific manual engineering, which does not scale. These abstractions are costly to generate and difficult to adjust or fine-tune. We instead propose a plug-and-play fix to automatically generate scene-specific, task-specific, adaptively updating abstractions on top of existing planning and control stacks. LLM-guided Environment Simplification (LENS) produces a de-cluttered abstracted scene representation by merging (e.g., stacked objects) or pruning (e.g., distant objects) scene entities in a closed loop in response to task progress. These dynamic, task-relevant abstractions are versatile and easy to use. In our experiments, we show that LENS improves classical planning, model-based control, and a vision-language-action model, across a diverse set of highly cluttered manipulation scenes. Project website: https://lens-2026.github.io/.

</details>


### [123] [Remote ID Spoofing-Aware Trajectory Planning for Small Unmanned Aerial Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19650)
*Jeremiah Webb,Bryce Bjorkman,Abel Diaz Gonzalez,Austin Coursey,Noah Dahle,Kailani Lemieux Mack,Filippos Fotiadis,Gautam Biswas,Bryan C. Ward,Abenezer Taye*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对RID位置欺骗攻击的去中心化、可欺骗感知的无人机轨迹规划框架。通过结合物理层信号强度检测欺骗并在规划中纳入不确定性，实现实时、分布式安全避碰。实验显示，对比传统方法能显著减少碰撞风险且具备实时性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无人机轨迹规划普遍假定Remote Identification（RID）数据可信，但在位置欺骗攻击下容易引发碰撞和安全风险，因此亟需能处理不可信RID信息的规划方法。

Method: 方法将RID信息视为未验证，并利用邻近飞机的接收信号强度检测欺骗，概率性定位欺骗源。将由此引入的不确定性通过机会约束法转化为风险边界，再结合基于马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）的去中心化轨迹规划，提升各自主避碰能力。

Result: 仿真包裹投递场景下，所提方法在多机环境下显著降低了近碰撞事件数，同时计算效率满足实时规划需求。

Conclusion: 通过集成物理层欺骗检测与机会约束规划，实现了鲁棒、可扩展的无人机避碰系统，在受RID欺骗威胁下也能有效维持安全与任务目标。

Abstract: This work presents a decentralized, spoofing-aware trajectory planning framework for small unmanned aerial systems operating under Remote Identification (RID) location spoofing attacks. Existing planners typically assume RID broadcasts are trustworthy, which can increase the risk of loss of separation and mid-air collisions when spoofing occurs. In contrast, the proposed approach explicitly treats RID information as unverified and incorporates physical-layer observations to assess broadcast credibility. Received signal-strength measurements from neighboring aircraft are used to detect spoofing and probabilistically localize a spoofing agent. The resulting uncertainty is converted into a risk-bounded unsafe region using a chance-constrained formulation and integrated into a per-agent Markov decision process-based planner. This enables real-time, decentralized collision avoidance while preserving mission objectives and scalability. Simulation results in a multi-aircraft package delivery scenario demonstrate reduced near mid-air collision events compared to planners that assume truthful RID data, while maintaining computational efficiency suitable for real-time execution.

</details>


### [124] [NavVerse: Benchmarking Indoor-to-Outdoor Embodied Navigation in Continuous Robot Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19695)
*Junzhe Wu,Yue Hu,Zeyu Han,Po-Hsun Chang,Yinan Dong,Behrad Rabiei,Maani Ghaffari*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了NavVerse，这是一个基于物理模拟的端到端室内到室外导航基准，填补了以往分离评估、忽略实际机器人执行与跨界适应的问题。实验显示目前方法距离解决跨场景导航任务仍有较大差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有导航基准多将室内与室外分开评测，并常常抽象掉机器人实际执行过程，导致对出口寻找、边界穿越、适应性与运动学 failures 等问题关注不足。实际应用如配送或应急响应中，机器人常需要跨越室内与室外，亟需更全面的基准环境。

Method: 作者构建了NavVerse基准，包含100个室内、50个城市室外与50个室内到室外场景，并在其中布置了多达1万个涵盖物体导航、视觉-语言导航和地点导航等任务的episode。代理需通过可执行的机器人接口完成场景中如寻找餐厅、银行等任务，并通过任务成功率、路径效率与安全性等指标进行评估。

Result: 在NavVerse上进行了零样本(Zero-shot)实验，包括强化学习（RL）、视觉-语言代理（VLA）、模块化等多种baseline。结果显示，现有方法对跨场景导航表现不佳。虽然端到端视觉-语言模型在零样本下成功率最高，模块化方法则在安全性上最优。地点导航任务进一步揭示从纯室外到“室内-室外”场景时性能显著下降，适应性为主要瓶颈。

Conclusion: NavVerse作为一个真实物理环境中的室内到室外导航基准，能更真实反映实际任务的挑战性。当前主流的导航方法还远不能应对复杂的跨场景任务，尤其在适应性方面表现薄弱，需进一步创新。

Abstract: Robots deployed in delivery, campus, and emergency-response settings often need to navigate from buildings to streets within a single continuous episode. Existing benchmarks usually evaluate indoor and outdoor navigation separately, and many abstract away robot execution, leaving exit finding, boundary traversal, adaptation, and kinodynamic failures underexplored. We introduce NavVerse, a physics-enabled benchmark for indoor-to-outdoor embodied navigation. NavVerse contains 100 indoor scenes, 50 urban outdoor scenes, and 50 indoor-to-outdoor scenes, and 10,000 episodes spanning Object Navigation, Vision-and-Language Navigation, and Place Navigation tasks, where agents search for semantic points of interest such as restaurants or banks. Agents are evaluated through executable robot interfaces using task-success, path-efficiency, and safety metrics. Zero-shot experiments with RL, VLA, and modular baselines show that current agents remain far from solving cross-context navigation: end-to-end VLAs obtain the highest zero-shot success, while the modular method provides the strongest safety profile. PlaceNav further reveals a clear drop from outdoor to indoor-to-outdoor scenes, indicating that adaptation remains major bottleneck.

</details>


### [125] [Contact-Persistent Full Actuation for Aerial Physical Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19708)
*Abhimanyu Khadga,Abhinav Sinha,Shashi Ranjan Kumar*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对无人机在持续接触任务下的全驱动能力判据，通过拓展全驱动的传统判别方法，更精确地评估无人机在物理交互任务中的残余控制能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统无人机全驱动能力的认证仅考虑空中自由飞行，而实际物理交互（如持续推、扶等）会消耗部分可用力矩，导致全驱动能力判据不全面，这可能影响无人机在实际任务下的安全和性能。

Method: 将三维空间刚体模型与考虑多种结构的力矩映射相结合，定义了有载荷时的可行力矩集与残余可行力矩集，提出了残余控制裕度作为更严格的全驱动能力标准，并通过多面体内外性理论分析能力边界。

Result: 理论证明了接触-持久全驱动能力等价于任务所需力矩在约束可行多面体内部，并提出了条件证书与鲁棒实现性标准。数值仿真表明，单纯的秩条件不足以保证接触任务可行性，且合适倾角有助于维持残余控制能力。

Conclusion: 秩条件并非无人机物理交互任务下全驱动能力的充分条件，应采用残余可行力矩分析和相关裕度标准来确认证书，更适用于安全关键和高性能的无人机物理交互场景。

Abstract: Fully actuated unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) are usually certified through rank conditions on a control-allocation matrix or through free-flight tracking performance. For aerial physical interaction, this certification may be incomplete. During sustained contact, part of the available wrench is consumed by the interaction task, and only the residual wrench remains available for stabilization, disturbance rejection, and maneuvering. This paper introduces a control-theoretic framework for \emph{contact-persistent full actuation}. A rigid-body model on $\R^{3}\times\SO\left(3\right)$ is combined with a morphology-dependent wrench map that captures fixed-tilt, variable-tilt, coaxial, and overactuated multirotor architectures. We define feasible wrench sets under actuator limits, residual wrench sets under task loading, and residual authority margins that strengthen the usual rank-based notion of full actuation. The main result shows that contact-persistent full actuation is equivalent to interiority of the task wrench in the constrained feasible wrench polytope, and that the residual authority radius is exactly the distance to the polytope boundary. We further introduce a signed residual-margin certificate for infeasible and boundary cases, a slack-maximizing allocation certificate, and a robust implementability condition that can be used as a margin-aware safety filter. Numerical evaluation on an abstract tilted hexarotor shows that full row rank alone does not imply feasible contact operation. Intermediate tilt angles preserve residual authority during pushing, whereas small or excessive tilts fail because of lateral-force deficiency or hover-margin loss.

</details>

To address this challenge, we present a cable-driven limbless robot that reconfigures body morphology and compliance to enable diverse locomotion modes. Distributed cable actuation generates traveling body waves, while programmable passive compliance enables robust contact-rich locomotion without terrain knowledge or high-bandwidth feedback. Rolling joints reorient bending planes along the body, enabling rapid reconfiguration and smooth transitions between locomotion styles, and incorporate geared locking to maintain configuration without continuous power. By combining programmable bending compliance and morphology control, the platform achieves lateral undulation, sidewinding, rolling, and twisting within a single system. Experiments demonstrate reliable gait generation, traversal in obstacle-rich environments, and transitions between modes, establishing a versatile limbless platform for navigating complex environments with applications in search and rescue, environmental monitoring, and inspection.

### [127] [EgoRecovery: Acquiring Failure Recovery Ability Through Human Recovery Demonstration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19745)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出EgoRecovery协同训练框架，安排人类在失败后高效采集恢复片段。通过将人类恢复演示对齐到与机器人共享的纠正意图空间，仅需少量机器人的恢复演示即可完成意图到机器动作的映射。部署时通过恢复门控机制，仅在需要纠正的状态激活恢复动作。

Result: 在现实环境的恢复任务实验显示，EgoRecovery在失败初始状态下的成功恢复率显著优于仅用机器人数据、直接协同训练和直接意图迁移等基线。

Abstract: Robust embodied robots should be able to recover from failures and retry tasks in order to operate reliably in unstructured and noisy real-world environments. Achieving this capability requires training policies on data that captures recovery behaviors. However, collecting such data through robot teleoperation is difficult to scale, as it is time-consuming to induce diverse failure states, perform corrective actions, and reset the environment. This challenge is further exacerbated by the high diversity of failure modes, which demands substantially more recovery data than success demonstrations. In this work, we show that egocentric human data capturing failure recovery processes provides a scalable alternative. By efficiently arranging task-level failure configurations and recording short recovery segments, human operators can generate more than 10x as much valid recovery data per hour compared to robot teleoperation under our protocol. To address the embodiment gap between human and robot, we propose EgoRecovery, a co-training framework for learning recovery behavior, where human recovery demonstrations are aligned to a compact corrective-intent space shared with robot data, which captures the timing and magnitude of correction. Only a small number of robot recovery demonstrations are required to connect this intent to executable robot actions. At deployment, a learned recovery gate predicts when correction is needed from robot observations and activates the corrective intent only in recovery states. Experiments on real-world recovery tasks show that EgoRecovery improves success from failure starts over robot-only recovery, direct co-training with human recovery data, and direct intent-transfer baselines.

Abstract: This paper presents a vision-informed grasp force prediction framework for robotic handling of date fruits. In this work, we develop a Vision-to-Force (V2F) pipeline that combines computer vision-based segmentation, active-contour refinement, and geometric feature extraction with a physics-informed residual neural network that augments a Hertz contact equation. The resulting model maps non-contact visual descriptors and cultivar metadata to predict a safe grasp force with mean validation performance of $R^2 \approx 0.7$ across unseen cultivar groups, which is a good result given the inherent mechanical variability of biological tissue. Experimental validation using a gripper and load cell indicates that the predicted forces enable stable manipulation of different types of date fruits, with residual deformations below 1 mm and no observable damage. These results show that pre-emptive, vision-driven force estimation% can replace slow and potentially damaging tactile exploration , enabling safer robotic handling of fragile fruits.

### [131] [SOPD-SocialNav: Selective On-Policy Distillation for Vision-Language Social Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19850)
*Xinyu Zhang,Zishuo Wang,Ling Xiao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前大规模视觉语言模型虽具备优秀的社交导航能力，但因算力需求大不易部署，而轻量化模型又因理解力弱难以胜任复杂社交环境导航，迫切需要高效知识迁移方法提升实用性。

Method: 提出Selective On-Policy Distillation（SOPD）方法，利用基于信息熵的机制筛选教师模型中关键决策token，并用温度控制的JS散度对学生与教师模型的分布在这些token上对齐，有效过滤无影响的梯度噪声，实现高效的社会导航知识迁移。

Result: 在SNEI和MUSON基准下，SOPD方法在行动预测、感知一致性和推理一致性等指标上均优于传统监督微调、离线蒸馏和标准在线蒸馏等方法。室外Scout Mini机器人测试进一步证明该模型能够生成更具社交适应性的导航行为。

Abstract: Vision-language models have shown strong potential for social robot navigation by leveraging rich semantic understanding of complex environments and human behaviors. However, large scale VLMs are difficult to deploy on resource-constrained robotic platforms, while lightweight VLMs often lack sufficient social reasoning capability. To address this problem, we propose SOPD-SocialNav, a selective on-policy distillation (SOPD) method that transfers social navigation knowledge from a large teacher VLM to a lightweight student VLM. SOPD introduces an entropy-based token selection mechanism that uses teacher uncertainty to identify socially informative decision tokens, while suppressing gradients from low-entropy tokens corresponding to trivial navigation states. A temperature-controlled Jensen-Shannon divergence objective is then used to align the student and teacher distributions on the selected tokens. Experiments on the SNEI and MUSON benchmarks demonstrate that SOPD consistently outperforms supervised fine-tuning, off-policy distillation, and standard on-policy distillation baselines in action prediction, perception consistency, and reasoning consistency. Real-world deployment on a Scout Mini robot further shows that the distilled model can generate more socially appropriate navigation behaviors in conversational and queuing scenarios. These results suggest that SOPD is an effective strategy for building lightweight yet socially aware VLM-based navigation systems.

### [132] [KineBench: Benchmarking Embodied World Models via IDM-Free Kinematic Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19876)
*Zeyu Liu,Zhangzhe Zhu,Yang Zhang,Chenyou Fan,Chenjia Bai,Xuelong Li*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了KineBench，一个不依赖逆动力学模型(IDM)的封闭环基准，用于更准确地评估具身世界模型(EWM)的物理一致性。其主要特征是直接从视频帧提取6D抓取器位姿进行物理仿真，并引入了新的运动学评价指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有EWMs的物理一致性评估主要依赖IDM闭环评测，但IDM对新颖场景很脆弱，易导致动作提取误差，进而混淆模型本身的能力与动作提取器失误，影响模型真实性能的评测。

Method: 作者提出KineBench，采用视觉基础模型Cascade提取每帧6D末端执行器位姿，摆脱IDM，通过物理仿真进行闭环验证。引入SPARC和Maruyama Manipulability等运动学指标，多维度评测轨迹平滑性和可行性。基于20个多样操作任务分为基础执行、任务迁移、视觉泛化和复杂度扩展四类评测套件。

Result: 基于KineBench的评测发现，在具身视频生成模型中，随着任务复杂度上升，模型表现存在非线性缩放，且对不同泛化与复杂度维度的能力有边界，揭示了当前前沿模型在数据扩展上的瓶颈。

Conclusion: KineBench有效减少了评测时的归因歧义，提升了具身世界模型的物理一致性评估准确性，并为未来模型扩展和数据策略的制定提供了实验依据和指导。

Abstract: Evaluating the physical consistency of embodied world models(EWMs) is a critical open challenge. While closed-loop evaluation via simulator rollouts offers a more faithful assessment of physical plausibility than open-loop alternatives, existing frameworks almost exclusively rely on Inverse Dynamics Models(IDMs) for action extraction. Due to the intricate mapping from 2D pixel space to 3D kinematic space, the learned IDMs can be brittle to data outside their training distribution, resulting in unreliable action extraction from the generated videos with novel objects and scenarios. This creates an unavoidable attribution ambiguity between world model inaccuracies and extractor errors. To reduce this ambiguity, we present KineBench, an IDM-free closed-loop benchmark for EWMs, built upon an explicit kinematic grounding pipeline. Given a generated video, KineBench employs cascaded visual foundation models to directly extract 6D end-effector poses from individual frames, which are then executed in a physics simulator for closed-loop validation. Beyond execution-based task success, KineBench incorporates two classical 3D kinematic metrics--Spectral Arc Length (SPARC) and the Maruyama Manipulability Index--to characterize trajectory smoothness and kinematic feasibility from a robot-centric perspective. Built on 20 diverse manipulation tasks in ManiSkill3, KineBench evaluates EWMs across four progressive suites: basic execution, task transfer, visual out-of-distribution generalization, and complexity-conditioned scaling. Evaluation across frontier models reveals task-complexity-bounded nonlinear scaling in embodied video generation, providing empirical guidance for future data-scaling strategies.

### [133] [EA-Nav: Learning Safe Visual Navigation Policies with Embodiment Awareness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19880)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Cross-embodiment navigation is a key challenge in embodied intelligence. Due to differences in embodiment, the same visual observation may imply different actions for different agents, making prediction ambiguous when relying solely on vision. Existing studies mainly rely on reinforcement learning, which requires large-scale interaction and careful reward design, making it difficult to support scalable pretraining and real-world adaptation. In contrast, imitation-learning-based approaches remain limited. To address these challenges, we propose an imitation-learning-based embodiment-aware navigation framework with a modular multi-stage design. In pretraining, we construct a cross-embodiment navigation dataset from Internet videos and introduce embodiment geometry as conditional tokens to reduce action ambiguity under the same observation. In fine-tuning, we design a multimodal information injection mechanism based on a decoupled architecture. Specifically, we design a trajectory augmentation strategy to generate high-risk samples, which are used to train spatial perception and risk-aware correction separately, thereby explicitly incorporating embodiment geometry for safe navigation. Experimental results show that the proposed method effectively improves navigation performance across different embodiment settings, demonstrating the effectiveness of incorporating embodiment geometry into embodied navigation.

</details>


### [134] [What Matters in Humanoid General Motion Tracking? An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19903)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 不同设计选择呈现出显著的分野，有些显著提升跟踪效果，有些主要影响执行能耗、训练复杂度或物理交互能力。YAHMP策略在真实G1上实现了多样化运动跟踪、抗外扰平衡及有力交互。

Abstract: Humanoid general motion tracking requires policies that can follow diverse whole-body references while maintaining balance. Building such policies involves many practical design choices, and their individual effects are often hard to assess. We address this issue with an empirical study of common modeling and training factors used in recent humanoid motion-imitation pipelines. To make the study controlled and reproducible, we developed YAHMP, an open-source modular framework for training, evaluating, and deploying whole-body motion tracking policies on the Unitree G1. Within YAHMP, we define a nominal configuration and compare variants that differ in motion-command representation, observation history, action representation, actuation profile, hand-force randomization during training, and training approach. We evaluate the resulting policies on a test set of retargeted human motions and compare the nominal policy with TWIST2 as an external baseline trained on the same motion set. The results distinguish choices with clear tracking effects from choices that mainly change actuation effort, training complexity, or physical interaction capability. Finally, we deploy YAHMP policies zero-shot on the real Unitree G1, demonstrating diverse whole-body motion tracking, balance under external perturbations, and forceful interaction.

### [135] [Diffusion ReRoll: Revisable Denoising for Robotic Sequential Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19919)
*Seonsoo Kim,Seongil Hong,Jun-Gill Kang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Diffusion ReRoll是一种可修正扩散预测框架，通过区域可重噪的方法，提升了机器人序列预测的表现，明显优于现有扩散方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前扩散法在序列生成上通常采用一次性、单调噪声消除，不便于对序列局部进行细致反复地修正，导致生成质量有限。希望改进扩散框架，使预测更灵活可修改，实现更高质量和一致性的机器人序列输出。

Method: 提出Diffusion ReRoll算法，在标准的扩散去噪进程下，检测局部已收敛稳定的区域，对其进行“重噪声”，从而允许利用剩余序列上下文信息进一步修正这些区域，支持跨区块的反复修正，实现序列生成过程的全局协调和局部一致性。

Result: 在OGBench PointMaze和AntMaze长时规划等任务中，Diffusion ReRoll平均成功率相较Diffusion Forcing提升21%，较Diffuser提升23%。在LIBERO-10多任务动作预测上，相较Diffusion Policy提升56.5%。在视频-动作联合建模中，有更好的一致性及鲁棒性，特别是在分布外测试下表现突出。

Conclusion: 结构化重噪声机制（structured re-noising）能有效提升机器人序列生成质量，实现可修正的生成过程，是扩散序列生成的有力改进。

Abstract: We propose Diffusion ReRoll, a diffusion-based framework for robotic sequential prediction that enables revisable denoising over horizons. Existing diffusion-based sequence predictors typically perform a single monotonic denoising process. In contrast, Diffusion ReRoll selectively re-noises regions that have become locally stable while the remaining regions continue denoising, so the re-noised regions can be refined again using context from the rest of the horizon. This structured re-noising enables iterative cross-horizon revision, allowing earlier and later segments to revise one another, while maintaining local consistency. We evaluate Diffusion ReRoll against full-sequence diffusion and causal denoising based on Diffusion Forcing across long-horizon planning, policy learning, and unified video-action modeling. On OGBench PointMaze and AntMaze, Diffusion ReRoll achieves relative gains in average success rate of 21% over Diffusion Forcing in matched guidance-based planning and 23% over Diffuser in matched goal-inpainting. In diffusion-policy-style action prediction, Diffusion ReRoll improves average success by 56.5% relative to Diffusion Policy across different prediction horizons and history lengths on the LIBERO-10 multi-task benchmark. In unified video-action prediction, Diffusion ReRoll improves policy and inverse dynamics performance, especially under out-of-distribution evaluation, and achieves the best action-video consistency. These results support structured re-noising as an effective mechanism for revisable robotic sequence generation.

*Taewon Seo,Seonae Jeon,Giwon Lee,Kuk-Jin Yoon,Daehee Park*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文针对机器人在人群密集环境中导航的场景，提出了一种有效解决多任务表示冲突的新框架，实现了运动预测与安全规划的高效统一模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前为人群社交机器人同时实现高效运动预测和安全轨迹规划，需要在资源受限设备上部署紧凑、统一的模型。然而，将两任务参数合并会导致表示冲突，影响模型性能。

Method: 作者提出了Disjoint Parameter Training (DPT) 框架，通过分离每项任务的关键参数区域并采用稀疏合并，仅融合最有影响力的参数，从而减少各任务之间的干扰。DPT能与多种参数合并方法并行适用。

Result: 在标准的人群导航基准（JRDB和JTA）上，所提出的DPT框架取得了优于现有方法的表现，展示了其高效性和通用性。

Conclusion: DPT有效缓解了统一模型中运动预测与安全规划的技能冲突，适合在资源受限的机器人平台部署，实现了更安全且节能的导航。

Abstract: Accurate motion prediction of surrounding agents and safe motion planning are two closely coupled key tasks for social robot navigation in crowded environments. Deploying these systems on resource-constrained edge devices necessitates compact, unified models that can perform both tasks simultaneously. However, within these compact shared encoders, recent unified models often overlook severe representational conflicts that arise from the distinct objectives of predicting neighbor behaviors versus ego-centric safety planning. To address this issue, we first identify the Skill Conflict$\unicode{x2014}$a phenomenon where overlapping parameter assignments cause distinct tasks to compete for the same weights, preventing the model from fully specializing in individual skills. To resolve this, we propose a novel model-merging-based framework, Disjoint Parameter Training (DPT). DPT mitigates performance degradation caused by Skill Conflict through distributed parameter learning, which separates the key parameter regions of each task while preserving their core capabilities prior to merging. In addition, we observe that sparse merging, which selectively integrates only the most influential parameters for each task rather than combining all task-specific parameters, yields optimal performance by preventing interference among adjacent features and concentrating representational capacity. DPT can be applied in parallel with a variety of merging methods. Evaluated on standard crowd navigation benchmarks (JRDB and JTA), our framework demonstrates superior performance, validating its versatility and effectiveness for safe, resource-efficient robot navigation.

### [137] [Robots Acquire Manipulation Skills in Seconds from a Single Human Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20033)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前机器人技能学习存在两个痛点：一是学习新技能过程慢、成本高；二是新技能训练常常导致旧技能遗忘。作者旨在解决机器人快速学习且稳定保留旧知识的问题。

Method: 提出HOST框架，核心思想是通过视频将人类演示映射到机器人任务进度，并通过预测未来观测来推断动作决策。利用自监督方式将视频进度和机器人轨迹映射到同一任务进度流形，并根据未来演示重新定义目标，使机器人主动模仿并自适应。

Result: HOST支持单视频秒级技能迁移（29秒），平均成功率62%。比零样本基线方法高45%，并在保留旧技能的同时，超过了需要50个演示样本微调的基线，训练效率提升507倍。

Conclusion: HOST使机器人能以极高的速度和极少数据从人类视频中获得新技能并保留旧技能，有望极大加速机器人自主学习的发展。

Abstract: The ability to acquire skills rapidly and effortlessly while retaining those already mastered is essential for robots. However, current methods still rely on a cumbersome training-time loop that is costly and slow, while eroding skills already mastered. In this paper, we introduce HOST (Human-to-robot One-Shot Skill AcquisiTion), a framework that enables a robot to acquire skills in seconds from a single human video while retaining previously mastered skills. HOST resolves skill acquisition through a cascade of self-grounded prediction. It first estimates the robot's progress within the demonstrated task, then translates the upcoming progression into the robot's own future observations, and finally derives actions from these predicted observations. This cascade is trained on targets coupled to the video demonstration, obtained by mapping the robot trajectory and the video demonstration onto a shared task progress manifold, then redefining each target to align with the future progression of the video. HOST thereby enables the robot to actively follow the demonstrated procedure and adapt it to the robot's embodiment. HOST acquires novel skills at inference time from a single human video in an average of 29 seconds and achieves a 62% average success rate. It exceeds the zero-shot baseline by 45% while retaining previously mastered skills. HOST even exceeds the baseline fine-tuned on 50 robot demonstrations per task while requiring 50 times fewer demonstrations and acquiring each skill 507 times faster. Additional information about HOST is available on the project website.

### [138] [ReferTrack: Referring Then Tracking for Embodied Visual Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20061)
*Hanjing Ye,Tianle Zeng,Jiazhao Zhang,Shaoan Wang,Zibo Zhang,Weisi Situ,Yuchen Zhou,Yonggen Ling,Hong Zhang*

TL;DR: 本文提出ReferTrack方法，用单目摄像头在视觉-语言-动作任务中更好地进行目标识别和跟踪，性能达SOTA并具备实际部署能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言-动作策略将目标识别与规划统一，但其推理往往在空间潜变量中进行，难以监督并与实际图像检测对齐，影响跟踪效果。

Method: 提出ReferTrack，采用referring-then-tracking范式：模型首先在候选框中选定目标，再结合图像信息推断跟踪轨迹。通过滑动窗口队列记录先前目标框的几何特征，以TVBI token形式注入历史视觉线索，并引入Refer-QA数据集联合训练增强识别能力。

Result: ReferTrack在EVT-Bench上取得单目性能SOTA，单目标、干扰、歧义跟踪子集成功率分别为89.4%、73.3%、74.1%，部分场景超越多相机方法。此外，在真实腿式及人形机器人平台上验证了仿真到现实的迁移能力。

Conclusion: ReferTrack通过显式目标定位与跟踪分离、时序视觉特征融合及多任务协同训练，实现了高效鲁棒的视觉跟踪能力，兼具理论先进性与实际应用价值。

Abstract: Embodied visual tracking (EVT) requires a mobile agent to continuously follow a specific target described in natural language using only onboard vision. While recent vision-language-action (VLA) policies unify target identification and trajectory planning, their chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning often operates in abstract spatial latents that are difficult to supervise and weakly aligned with explicit image-space detections. To address this, we introduce ReferTrack, a referring-then-tracking paradigm that grounds EVT using a single forward-facing camera. Our model first selects the target from an indexed set of bounding boxes, then decodes tracking waypoints conditioned on this image-grounded decision. To preserve target motion cues over time, ReferTrack maintains a sliding-window queue of previously selected bounding boxes, injecting their geometric features into the visual history via temporal-viewpoint-bbox indicator (TVBI) tokens. We further enhance target identification by co-training on a custom Refer-QA dataset. On EVT-Bench, ReferTrack achieves state-of-the-art single-view performance with success rates of 89.4%, 73.3%, and 74.1% on the single-target, distracted, and ambiguity tracking splits, respectively -- matching or even surpassing several multi-camera baselines on identification-heavy tasks. Finally, real-world deployments on legged and humanoid robots validate its robust sim-to-real transfer capabilities. Code is available at https://github.com/MedlarTea/referTrack.

Method: Extreme-RGMT采用两阶段的持续学习框架：首先利用多源数据训练通用的动作跟踪基础策略，之后通过不对称技能习得与能力巩固机制，对已掌握动作加以约束防止策略漂移，同时将学习重点放在难以完成的高动态片段。为解决高动态动作样本稀缺、失败率高、关键信息样本不足等问题，Extreme-RGMT结合了难度感知采样和优势优先的轨迹重采样方法，重点强化关键片段的训练。

Abstract: Humans can progressively acquire highly dynamic motor skills while preserving reliable everyday motor abilities. In contrast, existing humanoid controllers face a trade-off between generalist and specialist capabilities: generalist motion tracking policies struggle to reliably execute rare highly dynamic motions, whereas specialist training can degrade previously acquired behaviors. We introduce Extreme-RGMT, a two-stage continual learning framework for robust generalist humanoid control. The method first learns a generalist motion-tracking base policy from diverse multi-source motion data, then employs an asymmetric skill acquisition and capability consolidation mechanism to constrain policy drift on mastered motions while emphasizing difficult dynamic segments. To address the scarcity of highly dynamic motions, their high failure rates, and the resulting shortage of informative samples, Extreme-RGMT combines difficulty-aware sampling with advantage-prioritized trajectory resampling to emphasize critical segments. Experiments show that Extreme-RGMT achieves state-of-the-art generalist whole-body motion-tracking performance, including substantially improved completion of challenging highly dynamic motions. The resulting controller directly executes diverse unseen highly dynamic motions under fixed references and online inertial motion-capture inputs, advancing generalist whole-body motion-tracking controllers toward highly dynamic motor capabilities at the human-expert level.

  <summary>Details</summary>
