### [141] [DINS-IO: Learned Inertial Odometry via Differentiable INS Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20232)
*Hao Qiao,Yan Wang,Jian Kuang,Xiaoji Niu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种无需位置标签、仅依赖原始IMU数据的惯性里程计（DINS-IO）自监督训练方法，并通过有限标注数据进行校准，在标准基准测试中效果优于或媲美全监督方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习惯性里程计的训练通常依赖高精度位置真值数据（如运动捕捉、视觉-惯性里程计或SLAM），这些数据获取成本高且难以大规模收集。

Method: 利用惯性导航系统（INS）的速度递推公式作为强有力的自监督先验，将速度的一致性约束转化为滑动窗口最小二乘问题并求解，残差作为自监督损失反向传播。网络在IMU频率下输出密集速度预测，自监督训练后再用少量带标签数据低秩微调（LoRA），实现速度的度量校准。

Result: 在标准惯性里程计基准上，DINS-IO用极少量标注数据微调后，表现可与完全有监督方法媲美甚至更优。

Conclusion: DINS-IO显著降低了惯性里程计对大规模高精度位置信息的依赖，实现了高效自监督惯性导航，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: The training of learned inertial odometry depends on dense, high-precision position ground truth from motion capture, visual-inertial odometry or SLAM, which is costly and hard to acquire at scale. We propose DINS-IO, which learns inertial odometry directly from raw IMU streams without position labels. Our key insight is that the strapdown INS velocity recursion is a strong, fully differentiable consistency prior: the predicted velocity, rotated into the navigation frame, must agree with the integrated specific force up to an unknown initial velocity and a constant accelerometer bias. We cast this constraint as a sliding-window least-squares problem with a globally shared bias, solve it in closed form, and use the solver residual as a self-supervised loss whose gradient flows back to the network through the analytic solution. To supply this per-sample constraint, we design a high-frequency network that emits dense body-frame velocity at the IMU rate. Since the self-supervised network learns consistent motion but its velocity is not yet metrically calibrated, we calibrate it to true metric velocity from a few labeled trajectories by directly supervising the predicted body-frame velocity and adapting only low-rank (LoRA) patches. On standard benchmarks, DINS-IO pretrained self-supervised and fine-tuned with a small fraction of labels matches or surpasses fully supervised baselines.

</details>


### [142] [Courteous Anticipation: Improving Long-Lived Task Planning in Persistent Shared Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20289)
*Md Ridwan Hossain Talukder,Roshan Dhakal,Elizabeth Phillips,Gregory J. Stein*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多机器人环境中的有礼让预期规划方法，能够同时考虑当前和未来任务的整体成本，相比传统和自私式规划显著降低了总成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的机器人任务规划器通常是逐步处理任务，缺乏对未来任务的前瞻，也未考虑他人的约束，导致终态影响后续任务，造成成本增加。为降低多机器人共享环境下的长期任务总成本，需要使机器人在当前行动时预见未来任务的影响。

Method: 本文提出“courteous anticipatory planning”，基于模型的规划器会提出候选方案，并选择在所有机器人的即时成本与预估未来成本总和最小化的方案。它利用每个机器人独立的成本预测模型，避免了联合展开的组合爆炸，仅需单独训练机器人估算器，可模块化增加新机器人。

Result: 在家居和餐厅两个典型PDDL环境下测试，结果显示该方法在两机器人家居环境下比传统和自私预期规划分别降低总成本10.43%和4.03%，在三机器人餐厅分别降低17.41%和13.24%。

Conclusion: 该方法显著提升了多机器人长期任务执行的效率及协调性，适合扩展与部署到不断变化的多机器人系统环境。

Abstract: We consider a task planning scenario in which robots sharing a persistent environment are assigned tasks one at a time from a held-out sequence. Standard task planners, lacking foresight of future tasks and inconsiderate of others' constraints, solve each task in isolation, leaving terminal states that increase future cost for all, side effects that compound over lengthy task sequences. To reduce cost over the sequence, a robot must anticipate how its actions now may impact performance on future tasks for all robots sharing the environment. Therefore, we present courteous anticipatory planning, wherein a model-based planner proposes candidate plans and selects the one that jointly minimizes immediate cost and aggregated expected future cost across all robots, estimated via independent per-robot learned estimators. This factored formulation avoids combinatorial joint rollouts and supports modular deployment: adding a robot requires only training its own estimator. We evaluate in two persistent PDDL domains, a home environment with robots that have similar capabilities but different responsibilities, and a restaurant environment where robots' distinct capabilities create states that other robots lack the capability to resolve. During lengthy task sequences, our planner reduces total cost by 10.43% versus myopic and 4.03% versus selfish anticipatory planning in a two-robot home environment and by 17.41% and 13.24%, respectively, in a three-robot restaurant.

</details>


### [143] [Closing the Lab-to-Store Gap: A Data-Efficient Post-Training and Experience-Driven Learning VLA Framework for Retail Humanoids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20345)
*Roger Sala Sisó,Tiago Silvério,Jakob Sand,Tran Nguyen Le*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为DEED的新系统，用于提升类人视觉-语言-动作（VLA）机器人在现实环境中的可靠性，主要验证于超市补货任务上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管VLA类人机器人在基准测试中表现良好，但在实际操作中因执行失误、分布转移和环境变化依然表现不佳，因此要求新的方法来缩小实验与真实环境间的差距。

Method: 提出了DEED系统，包括三大部分：（1）高效的数据后训练流程，通过控制频率对齐、数据筛选、视觉高亮和降低对VLA依赖，提升效率和泛化能力；（2）借鉴RECAP方法、引入文本前缀优势和视觉语言价值函数的真实环境经验驱动学习；（3）开发潜空间分析工具，用以评估模型在分布内外的行为表现。

Result: 实验证明，通过DEED的数据和系统优化，原本依赖简单微调效果很差的策略，可以仅用单块GPU变为适应现实场景的高效系统。系统性集成优于单纯模型架构创新。

Conclusion: 将类人VLA机器人从实验环境推广到真实世界，核心限制在于系统集成与数据处理，而非模型结构本身。DEED能显著提升实际应用表现，验证了系统层面改进的重要性。

Abstract: Closing the gap between benchmark performance and reliable real-world operation remains a central challenge for Vision-Language-Action (VLA) humanoid robots, which must handle execution errors, distribution shifts, and environmental variability. This paper presents DEED (Data-Efficient Post-Training and Experience-Driven Learning), a systems-level approach evaluated on a supermarket chip-restocking task using a Unitree G1-Edu humanoid robot and the GR00T N1.6 foundation model. DEED comprises three key components: (1) a data-efficient post-training pipeline with control-frequency alignment, data curation, task-relevant visual highlighting, and reduced VLA dependence; (2) a real-world study of experience-driven refinement, adapted from RECAP via a text-based advantage prefix and a vision-language value function; and (3) a latent-space analysis tool for studying in- and out-of-distribution behavior. Our results suggest that bridging the lab-to-store gap is primarily a systems integration challenge rather than an architectural one: careful data design and targeted post-training can transform a policy that fails under naive fine-tuning into a competent real-world system using only a single GPU.

</details>


### [144] [Distributed Motion Planning with Safety Guarantees for Self-Reconfiguring Robotic Boats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20352)
*Alejandro Gonzalez-Garcia,Wei Wang,Wei Xiao,Wilm Decre,Jan Swevers,Carlo Ratti,Daniela Rus*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合分布式模型预测控制（MPC）与控制障碍函数（CBF）的水下多机器人协作组形框架，实现安全高效的队形构建和重组，并通过仿真和实物实验验证了方法的有效性与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水下多机器人协作需要在保证安全交互的同时，实现灵活、高效的队形构建和重组。现有方法常因优化问题的非凸性和安全约束难以兼顾，影响系统的性能和实用性。为了解决这一挑战，本文提出新的控制框架。

Method: 该方法将分布式MPC和CBF有机结合。通过ADMM求解实现分布式MPC，协同规划多机器人轨迹；实时采用CBF保证多主体间的碰撞避免。MPC负责预测与规避局部最优，CBF则为安全性提供理论保障。

Result: 仿真中系统可支持多至25个机器人协作，实验中使用四台实物机器人完成任务，验证了方法的有效性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 所提框架可高效且安全地实现多机器人水下组形任务，为类似多主体系统的安全协作控制提供了新思路。

Abstract: Aquatic self-reconfigurable robots must assemble into desired shapes while ensuring safe interactions among multiple agents. This paper proposes a hybrid framework that combines distributed Model Predictive Control (MPC) with Control Barrier Functions (CBFs) for multi-agent shape formation and reconfiguration. Given a desired shape and target assignment, a distributed MPC scheme, solved via the Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM), computes coordinated trajectories through local optimization and information exchange. To ensure safety in real time, distributed CBF-based filters are applied to enforce inter-agent collision avoidance. The proposed approach leverages the predictive capabilities of MPC to mitigate local minima, while CBFs provide formal safety guarantees despite the nonconvexity of the underlying optimization problem. Simulation results with up to 25 agents and experimental validation with four physical robots demonstrate the effectiveness and scalability of the framework.

</details>


### [145] [Distributed Acoustic Localization Array Deployed Using a Soft Everting Vine Robot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20392)
*Sebastian Lorca Godoy,Ciera McFarland,Michael Val,Antonio Alvarez Valdivia,Nathaniel Hanson,Margaret McGuinness*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种基于声音的软体伸展机器人外部感知系统，用于狭小和复杂环境下对灾害受困者的定位。通过沿藤蔓式软体机器人体布置分布式麦克风阵列，结合动态声源定位算法，在不同结构和信噪比条件下实现了高精度的三维声源定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 灾害救援环境结构复杂，传统硬质机器人难以进入受限空间且受困者定位难。软体机器人能适应狭小和不规则环境，因此设计特定的外部感知系统对灾害受困者的实时精准定位有现实意义。

Method: 采用分布式声学传感体系，将五麦克风阵列布置在软体机器人不同部位（身体内部、尾部、外壁），测试多种机器人形态（线性、环状等）、信噪比、接近方向等变量下，基于Steered Response Power with Phase Transform算法实现远近场三维定位。机器人在变形生长过程中，动态收集声源信息。

Result: 无论麦克风阵列在机器人表面何处布置，哪怕只有三只麦克风被推出外壁，也能实现高精度的近场声源定位。实验表明，在不同配置及噪声条件下，定位精度依然可靠。

Conclusion: 分布式声学感知结合软体伸展机器人，能够在复杂灾害环境中高效、可靠地完成对受困者的声学定位，展示了软体机器人在实际救援场景中的巨大应用潜力。

Abstract: Soft robot exteroception is increasingly being explored for a variety of field applications. In this work, we present a sound-based system for localizing disaster victims in confined and unstructured environments, based on a distributed acoustic sensing architecture embedded along the body of a soft everting vine robot. We propose a dynamic Steered Response Power with Phase Transform framework that supports both far-field direction-of-arrival estimation and near-field three-dimensional source localization as the robot approaches the sound source. To better understand the design and control space related to localizing sound using a soft, shape-morphing robot body, we conduct experiments measuring the accuracy of these methods for a five-microphone array attached to the robot body using three placements relative to the outer membrane of the robot (inside the pressurized body, inside the inner tail, and outside the outer wall) and in four robot configurations (linear, double linear, circular, and sinusoidal). We measure the change in accuracy as the signal-to-noise ratio, the direction of approach, and the distance of the sound source from the center of the array change. Finally, we demonstrate a vine robot growing into an arbitrary shape while carrying microphones along its outer wall, and show that a sound source located with the array's near field can be localized with high accuracy after only three microphones have everted from the robot body. These results highlight the potential of distributed acoustic sensing for reliable victim localization using soft growing robots.

</details>


### [146] [Towards Miniature Humanoid Tele-Loco-Manipulation Using Virtual Reality and Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20399)
*Nicolas Kosanovic,Jordan Dowdy,Jean Chagas Vaz*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文开发了一套完整的远程实时控制系统，使得小型类人机器人能够实现自主行走和操控，并通过实验展示了其实用性和高效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前全尺寸类人机器人虽已可以在实际人类环境中由远程操作，但价格昂贵，设备复杂，难以普及。小型类人机器人虽然普及率高，但控制方式落后、仿生性差，缺乏匹配的远程操控解决方案。

Method: 从零设计了适用于小型类人机器人的柔顺全身远程操作控制系统。上半身由虚拟现实实现遥操作，下半身采用强化学习算法实现平衡与行走，在ROBOTIS OP3平台上进行了实证测试，包括步行测试和搬运实验。

Result: 在ROBOTIS OP3硬件上系统实现了独立于手臂动作的0.45 m/s步行速度。通过专家远程操作，实验中10分钟内平均可移动2个40克立方体，总步行5米，展示了系统的有效性。

Conclusion: 该系统为小型类人机器人提供了实用的全身远程操控方案，具有良好的运动和操作能力，验证了小型机器人在远程人机协作和物体搬运方面的潜力。

Abstract: Full-sized humanoid robot capabilities have grown exponentially in recent years, aiming towards general-purpose deployment in human environments. A popular control method used by manufacturers utilizes Virtual Reality for upper-body teleoperation and Reinforcement Learning for lower-body balance and locomotion control. As a result, a single remote operator can see, manipulate, and navigate about a real, distant physical environment. This powerful control stack is often relegated to expensive full-sized robots, many of which are inaccessible to the research community. Miniature humanoids are more prevalent, but employ less biomimicry in their design (e.g. fewer sensors, Degrees of Freedom, etc) and lack similar developments. This paper describes a compliant full-body telepresence control stack developed from the ground up for miniature humanoids. Framework experimentation on ROBOTIS OP3 hardware showcases walking at speeds up to 0.45 m/s independent of arm motions. Tele-loco-manipulation is demonstrated via a cube relocation experiment with an expert human operator. On average, the teleoperated system moved 2 different 40 g cubes within 10 mins, walking a total distance of 5 m. Overall, the developed system shows potential for miniature humanoid tele-loco-manipulation.

</details>
